SUBENT        C1038001   20140924                             C145C103800100001 
BIB                 15         46                                 C103800100002 
TITLE      Production of Neutrons with Protons of 22, 30, and 40  C103800100003 
           MeV in Stopping Targets of Carbon, Aluminum, Copper,   C103800100004 
           Silver, Tantalum, and Lead                             C103800100005 
AUTHOR     (T.M.Amos,R.R.Doering,A.Galonsky,R.Jolly,M.K.Zigrang)  C103800100006 
REFERENCE  (J,NSE,147,73,2004)                                    C103800100007 
           (T,AMOS,1972) Michigan State University.               C103800100008 
EXP-YEAR   (1970)                                                 C103800100009 
INSTITUTE  (1USAMSU)                                              C103800100010 
FACILITY   (ISOCY,1USAMSU)                                        C103800100011 
INC-SPECT  Incident protons with energies 22 - 40 MeV.            C103800100012 
SAMPLE     Each target was a cylinder 2.54 cm in diameter and of  C103800100013 
           thickness equal to the proton range in each material;  C103800100014 
           there was a set of six targets for each proton         C103800100015 
           bombarding energy.                                     C103800100016 
DETECTOR   (SCIN) NE-213 liquid scintillator encapsulated in a    C103800100017 
           cylinder of glass with inside dimensions of 4.44-cm    C103800100018 
           diameter by 1.90-cm thickness.                         C103800100019 
PART-DET   (N,G)                                                  C103800100020 
METHOD     (BCINT,PSD,TOF) The plan of the measurements was to    C103800100021 
           detect and determine the energies of the neutron       C103800100022 
           emitted at 0, 30, 60, 90, 120, and 150 degrees. The    C103800100023 
           following techniques were used: TOF to determine       C103800100024 
           neutron energy, pulse- shape-discrimination to         C103800100025 
           separate neutron-induced pulses from gamma-ray-        C103800100026 
           induced pulses, and flight path of two different       C103800100027 
           lengths to cover a large neutron energy range with     C103800100028 
           good resolution. Faraday cup was used to determine     C103800100029 
           the number of incident protons during each run.        C103800100030 
CORRECTION Plotted data corrections were made for dead time of    C103800100031 
           the electronics and for interactions of the neutrons   C103800100032 
           within the stopping targets. Depending on beam         C103800100033 
           intensity and neutron yield, the dead time             C103800100034 
           corrections were in the range of 5 to 15 %.            C103800100035 
           Corrections for neutron interactions were more         C103800100036 
           complex, but the results were of no greater magnitude. C103800100037 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-T) Combing all errors in quadratures gives a      C103800100038 
           final error of approximately +-15 %.                   C103800100039 
           (ERR-1,5.,15.) Dead time corrections.                  C103800100040 
           (ERR-2) Reduced number of neutrons reaching the        C103800100041 
           detector due to in scattering from neighboring parts.  C103800100042 
           (ERR-3) Neutron detection efficiency.                  C103800100043 
           (ERR-4) Data merging error.                            C103800100044 
STATUS     (APRVD) Approved by A. Galonsky, 2004/6/30.            C103800100045 
HISTORY    (20040629C) VM                                         C103800100046 
           (20140924A) BP: Updated the entry, added thesis data,  C103800100047 
           error-analysis, and digitized thesis Figs. 25-27, 32.  C103800100048
